	-- Hydra.Wait(2.0)
	Hydra.QActorPlayConversation(convErvin00a, idSelf, idErvin00)
	-- Hydra.Wait(3.0)
	Hydra.SetPlayerVariableFlag(idSelf, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_ErvinSaved")
	idErvinClone = Hydra.CreatePersonalClone(idErvin00, true)
	if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idErvinClone) then
		Hydra.QActorClearAnimSetOverride(idErvinClone)
		-- move Ervin to resting loc
		Hydra.QActorWait(idErvinClone, 1.0)
		Hydra.QActorPlayConversation(convErvin00b, idSelf, idErvinClone)
		Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(idErvinClone, idErvin02, "NPC_Walk", true)
		Hydra.QActorFaceSameAsActor(idErvinClone, idErvin02, true)
		Hydra.QActorDeletePersonalClone(idErvinClone)
	end
	
	-- Hydra.ActorDisableAI(idErvin01)
	
	-- Hydra.QActorFadeAndDelete(idErvin01, 0.5)
	
	-- Hydra.WaitForQEmpty(idErvinClone)
	Hydra.EventSend("DeadintheWater_ErvinResting", idSelf)
end

	-- this event previously sent at end of this callback:
	Hydra.EventSend("DeadintheWater_BodyBurned", idSelf)
	
	if Hydra.ItemGetCount(idSelf, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_Salvage") < 10 then
	
		Hydra.ItemDropAtActor(idSelf, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_Salvage")
		
	end
	-- use this to check as condition on On Enter
	-- if true, set Body01Burned as well
	Hydra.SetPlayerVariableFlag(idActor, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_Body01Looted")
	-- wait a beat for flippy anim
	Hydra.Wait(1.0)
	
	-- TODO: Tomaj anim actions and return to follower
	local idTomajFollower = Hydra.QuestGetFollower("NPC_QST_Hawe_Tomaj_Follower")
	--  - set Tomaj actively burning var to true
	Hydra.SetPlayerVariableFlag(idActor, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_TomajBurning")
	
	if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idTomajFollower) then
		--  - have Tomaj kneel or "lean over" next to corpse
		Hydra.ActorDisableAI(idTomajFollower)
		Hydra.QActorStopAllQueuedActions(idTomajFollower)
		Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(idTomajFollower, idTomaj01a, "NPC_Run", false)
		Hydra.QActorFaceActor(idTomajFollower, idTomaj01a, true)
		Hydra.QActorPhasedAnimLoop(idTomajFollower, "AnimKey_Use_Crouch", 3)
		Hydra.Wait(5.0)
	
		-- if follower still valid, after the Hydra.Wait
		if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idTomajFollower) then
			if Hydra.GetPlayerVariableNumericValue(idActor, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_BodiesBurned") == 0 then
				Hydra.QActorPlayConversation(convTomaj04b, idActor, idTomajFollower)
			end
			--  - reenable Tomaj as follower
			Hydra.ActorEnableAI(idTomajFollower)
		end
	end
	--  - set Tomaj actively burning var to false
	Hydra.ResetPlayerVariable(idActor, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_TomajBurning")
	
	-- set unique-to-body player variable
	Hydra.SetPlayerVariableFlag(idActor, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_Body01Burned")
	
	-- original location of repeatable body user event:
	-- Hydra.EventSend("DeadintheWater_BodyBurned", idSelf)

end

		Hydra.ActorDisableAI(idTomajFollower)
		Hydra.QActorStopAllQueuedActions(idTomajFollower)
		Hydra.QActorMoveToLocationDynamicSpeed(idTomajFollower, idTomaj01c, "NPC_Run", false)
		Hydra.QActorFaceActor(idTomajFollower, idTomaj01c, true)
		Hydra.QActorPhasedAnimLoop(idTomajFollower, "AnimKey_Use_Crouch", 3)
		Hydra.Wait(5.0)
	
		-- if follower still valid, after the Hydra.Wait
		if Hydra.ActorIsValid(idTomajFollower) then
			if Hydra.GetPlayerVariableNumericValue(idActor, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_BodiesBurned") == 0 then
				Hydra.QActorPlayConversation(convTomaj04b, idActor, idTomajFollower)
			end
			--  - reenable Tomaj as follower
			Hydra.ActorEnableAI(idTomajFollower)
		end
	end
	
	--  - set Tomaj actively burning var to false
	Hydra.ResetPlayerVariable(idActor, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_TomajBurning")
	
	-- set unique-to-body player variable
	Hydra.SetPlayerVariableFlag(idActor, "QST_Hawe_DeadintheWater_Body03Burned")
	
	-- original location of repeatable body user event:
	-- Hydra.EventSend("DeadintheWater_BodyBurned", idSelf)
end

	Hydra.QActorDelete(idErvinFollower)
